	$(document).ready(function() {

			    		siteorder ="3";
			    	}else if(dataMap.gubun == 'ETC'){
			    		sitename ="";
			    		siteorder ="4";
			    	}else if(dataMap.gubun == 'DO'){
			    		sitename ="//";
			    		siteorder ="5";
			    	}
			    	if(i == 0){
			    		innerHtml +='<ul class="width-auto clearfix">';
			    	}
			    	if(dataMap.grpstt == dataMap.orgorder){
			    		innerHtml +='	<li><a href="#none" class="open"><span>'+sitename+'</span></a>';
		    			innerHtml +='		<div class="footer-floor1-con absolute'+siteorder+'">';
    					innerHtml +='			<ul class="clearfix">';
			    	}

			    	if(dataMap.grpend == dataMap.orgorder){
			    		innerHtml +='			</ul>';
			    		innerHtml +='		</div>';
			    		innerHtml +='		<a href="#none" class="c5_close out"><img src="/files/web148/images/main/btn_close_sitemap.png" alt="'+sitename+'  " /></a>';
			    		innerHtml +='	</li>';				    					
			    	}
					if(i == data.list.length){
						innerHtml +='</ul>';
			    	}
			    }
			    $(".footer-floor1").html(innerHtml);
			    loadJQuery();//     layout.js  
		    }
	    });
	});
	function loadJQuery() {
		$('.footer-floor1 > ul > li > .open').on('click', function(){
			$(this).removeAttr('href');
			var elem = $(this).parent('li');
			if (elem.hasClass('on')) {
				elem.removeClass('on');
				elem.find('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.find('div').slideUp();
			}
			else {
				elem.addClass('on');
				elem.children('div').slideDown();
				elem.siblings('li').children('div').slideUp();
				elem.siblings('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.siblings('li').find('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.siblings('li').find('div').slideUp();
			}
		});

		$('a.c5_close.out').click(function(){
			$(this).parents("li").removeClass("on");
		});

		$(".m-dp3-area-right-floor2 a").focus(function(){
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});

		$(".opinion a").focus(function(){
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});


		$(".c5_close").click(function(){
			$(this).attr("href","#none");
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
			$(this).parent().next().find('.open').focus();
			if ( $(this).hasClass('last') ){
				$('.btm-logo > a').focus();
				$(this).hide();
			}
		});
		$(".c5_close").blur(function(){
			$(this).attr("href","#none");
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});
		$('.btm-logo > a').focus(function(){
			$('.c5_close').hide();		
		});
	}
</script>

	<script>
	function ssetCookie( name, value, expirehours ) {
		var todayDate = new Date();
		todayDate.setHours( todayDate.getHours() + expirehours );
	  	document.cookie = name + "=" + escape( value ) + "; path=/; expires=" + todayDate.toGMTString() + ";";
	}
	
	function ccloseWin(popupid) {
		ssetCookie("ncookie"+popupid, "done" , 24 );	
		$("#ncookie"+popupid).hide();
	}
	
	
	
  	function ggetCookie(popupid) {
		cookiedata = document.cookie;
	 	var checkcookie = popupid+"=done";
	 	if (cookiedata.indexOf(checkcookie) > -1){
		 	$("#ncookie"+popupid).hide();
	 	} else {
		 	$("#ncookie"+popupid).show();
	 	}
	}
	</script>

	$(document).ready(function() {
		var innerHtml = "";
		var sitename = "";
		var siteorder = "";
		cityGuideService.getHomePageSearch('', function(data) {
		    var dataLength = data.list.length;
		    if (dataLength > 0) {
			    for (var i = 0; i < data.list.length; i++) {
			    	var dataMap = data.list[i];
			    	if(dataMap.gubun == 'KUK'){
			    		sitename ="";
			    		siteorder ="1";
			    	}else if(dataMap.gubun == 'DONG'){
			    		sitename ="";
			    		siteorder ="2";
			    	}else if(dataMap.gubun == 'SI'){
			    		sitename ="";
			    		siteorder ="3";
			    	}else if(dataMap.gubun == 'ETC'){
			    		sitename ="";
			    		siteorder ="4";
			    	}else if(dataMap.gubun == 'DO'){
			    		sitename ="//";
			    		siteorder ="5";
			    	}
			    	if(i == 0){
			    		innerHtml +='<ul class="width-auto clearfix">';
			    	}
			    	if(dataMap.grpstt == dataMap.orgorder){
			    		innerHtml +='	<li><a href="#none" class="open"><span>'+sitename+'</span></a>';
		    			innerHtml +='		<div class="footer-floor1-con absolute'+siteorder+'">';
    					innerHtml +='			<ul class="clearfix">';
			    	}
			    	innerHtml +='					<li><a href="' + dataMap.homelink + '" target="_blank">' + dataMap.orgname + '</a></li>';
			    	if(dataMap.grpend == dataMap.orgorder){
			    		innerHtml +='			</ul>';
			    		innerHtml +='		</div>';
			    		innerHtml +='		<a href="#none" class="c5_close out"><img src="/files/web148/images/main/btn_close_sitemap.png" alt="'+sitename+'  " /></a>';
			    		innerHtml +='	</li>';				    					
			    	}
					if(i == data.list.length){
						innerHtml +='</ul>';
			    	}
			    }
			    $(".footer-floor1").html(innerHtml);
			    loadJQuery();//     layout.js  
		    }
	    });
	});
	function loadJQuery() {
		$('.footer-floor1 > ul > li > .open').on('click', function(){
			$(this).removeAttr('href');
			var elem = $(this).parent('li');
			if (elem.hasClass('on')) {
				elem.removeClass('on');
				elem.find('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.find('div').slideUp();
			}
			else {
				elem.addClass('on');
				elem.children('div').slideDown();
				elem.siblings('li').children('div').slideUp();
				elem.siblings('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.siblings('li').find('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.siblings('li').find('div').slideUp();
			}
		});

		$('a.c5_close.out').click(function(){
			$(this).parents("li").removeClass("on");
		});

		$(".m-dp3-area-right-floor2 a").focus(function(){
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});

		$(".opinion a").focus(function(){
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});


		$(".c5_close").click(function(){
			$(this).attr("href","#none");
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
			$(this).parent().next().find('.open').focus();
			if ( $(this).hasClass('last') ){
				$('.btm-logo > a').focus();
				$(this).hide();
			}
		});
		$(".c5_close").blur(function(){
			$(this).attr("href","#none");
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});
		$('.btm-logo > a').focus(function(){
			$('.c5_close').hide();		
		});
	}
</script>

	<script>
	function ssetCookie( name, value, expirehours ) {
		var todayDate = new Date();
		todayDate.setHours( todayDate.getHours() + expirehours );
	  	document.cookie = name + "=" + escape( value ) + "; path=/; expires=" + todayDate.toGMTString() + ";";
	}
	
	function ccloseWin(popupid) {
		ssetCookie("ncookie"+popupid, "done" , 24 );	
		$("#ncookie"+popupid).hide();
	}
	
	
	
  	function ggetCookie(popupid) {
		cookiedata = document.cookie;
	 	var checkcookie = popupid+"=done";
	 	if (cookiedata.indexOf(checkcookie) > -1){
		 	$("#ncookie"+popupid).hide();
	 	} else {
		 	$("#ncookie"+popupid).show();
	 	}
	}

  	function weather_timeline3() {
		$.ajax({
	  	    url : "/app/weather_timeline3.jsp",
	  	    type : "post",
	  	    async : false,
	  	    cache : false,
	  	    success : function(data) {
				if ($.trim(data) != "") {
	  	        	$(".weather").html(data);
	  	      	}
			},
  	    	error : function(e) {
				alert(e.responseText);
  	    	}
  	  	});
  	}

	function getCookie2(emgwordid) {
		cookiedata = document.cookie;
		 var checkcookie = emgwordid+"=done";
		 if (cookiedata.indexOf(checkcookie) > -1){
			 $("#topmost_corona").hide();
		 } else {
			 $("#topmost_corona").show();
		 }
	}
	
	function setCookie( name, value, expirehours ) {
		if($("input:checkbox[id='chk_today']").is(":checked") == true){
			var todayDate = new Date();
			todayDate.setHours( todayDate.getHours() + expirehours );
		  	document.cookie = name + "=" + escape( value ) + "; path=/; expires=" + todayDate.toGMTString() + ";";
		}
	}
	
	function closeWin(emgwordid) {
		if(emgwordid == "topmost_corona"){//jdh  
			setCookie("topmost_corona", "done" , 24 );
		}else{
			setCookie("emgpopupcookie"+emgwordid, "done" , 24 );	
		}
	   	
	 }

	$(document).ready(function() {

		cityGuideService.getHomePageSearch('', function(data) {
		    var dataLength = data.list.length;
		    if (dataLength > 0) {
			    for (var i = 0; i < data.list.length; i++) {
			    	var dataMap = data.list[i];

			    		siteorder ="1";
			    	}else if(dataMap.gubun == 'DONG'){
			    		sitename ="";
			    		siteorder ="2";
			    	}else if(dataMap.gubun == 'SI'){
			    		sitename ="";
			    		siteorder ="3";
			    	}else if(dataMap.gubun == 'ETC'){
			    		sitename ="";
			    		siteorder ="4";
			    	}else if(dataMap.gubun == 'DO'){
			    		sitename ="//";
			    		siteorder ="5";
			    	}
			    	if(i == 0){
			    		innerHtml +='<ul class="width-auto clearfix">';
			    	}
			    	if(dataMap.grpstt == dataMap.orgorder){

		    			innerHtml +='		<div class="footer-floor1-con absolute'+siteorder+'">';

			    		innerHtml +='			</ul>';
			    		innerHtml +='		</div>';
			    		innerHtml +='		<a href="#none" class="c5_close out"><img src="/files/web148/images/main/btn_close_sitemap.png" alt="'+sitename+'  " /></a>';
			    		innerHtml +='	</li>';				    					
			    	}
					if(i == data.list.length){
						innerHtml +='</ul>';
			    	}
			    }
			    $(".footer-floor1").html(innerHtml);
			    loadJQuery();//     layout.js  
		    }
	    });
	});
	function loadJQuery() {
		$('.footer-floor1 > ul > li > .open').on('click', function(){
			$(this).removeAttr('href');
			var elem = $(this).parent('li');
			if (elem.hasClass('on')) {
				elem.removeClass('on');
				elem.find('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.find('div').slideUp();
			}
			else {
				elem.addClass('on');
				elem.children('div').slideDown();
				elem.siblings('li').children('div').slideUp();
				elem.siblings('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.siblings('li').find('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.siblings('li').find('div').slideUp();
			}
		});

		$('a.c5_close.out').click(function(){
			$(this).parents("li").removeClass("on");
		});

		$(".m-dp3-area-right-floor2 a").focus(function(){
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});

		$(".opinion a").focus(function(){
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});


		$(".c5_close").click(function(){
			$(this).attr("href","#none");
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
			$(this).parent().next().find('.open').focus();
			if ( $(this).hasClass('last') ){
				$('.btm-logo > a').focus();
				$(this).hide();
			}
		});
		$(".c5_close").blur(function(){
			$(this).attr("href","#none");
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});
		$('.btm-logo > a').focus(function(){
			$('.c5_close').hide();		
		});
	}
</script>

	<script>
	function ssetCookie( name, value, expirehours ) {
		var todayDate = new Date();
		todayDate.setHours( todayDate.getHours() + expirehours );
	  	document.cookie = name + "=" + escape( value ) + "; path=/; expires=" + todayDate.toGMTString() + ";";
	}
	
	function ccloseWin(popupid) {
		ssetCookie("ncookie"+popupid, "done" , 24 );	
		$("#ncookie"+popupid).hide();
	}
	
	
	
  	function ggetCookie(popupid) {
		cookiedata = document.cookie;
	 	var checkcookie = popupid+"=done";
	 	if (cookiedata.indexOf(checkcookie) > -1){
		 	$("#ncookie"+popupid).hide();
	 	} else {
		 	$("#ncookie"+popupid).show();
	 	}
	}

  	function weather_timeline3() {
		$.ajax({
	  	    url : "/app/weather_timeline3.jsp",
	  	    type : "post",
	  	    async : false,
	  	    cache : false,
	  	    success : function(data) {
				if ($.trim(data) != "") {
	  	        	$(".weather").html(data);
	  	      	}
			},
  	    	error : function(e) {
				alert(e.responseText);
  	    	}
  	  	});
  	}

	function getCookie2(emgwordid) {
		cookiedata = document.cookie;
		 var checkcookie = emgwordid+"=done";
		 if (cookiedata.indexOf(checkcookie) > -1){
			 $("#topmost_corona").hide();
		 } else {
			 $("#topmost_corona").show();
		 }
	}
	
	function setCookie( name, value, expirehours ) {
		if($("input:checkbox[id='chk_today']").is(":checked") == true){
			var todayDate = new Date();
			todayDate.setHours( todayDate.getHours() + expirehours );
		  	document.cookie = name + "=" + escape( value ) + "; path=/; expires=" + todayDate.toGMTString() + ";";
		}
	}
	
	function closeWin(emgwordid) {
		if(emgwordid == "topmost_corona"){//jdh  
			setCookie("topmost_corona", "done" , 24 );
		}else{
			setCookie("emgpopupcookie"+emgwordid, "done" , 24 );	
		}
	   	
	 }

			    		sitename ="";

			    		sitename ="//";
			    		siteorder ="5";

			    		innerHtml +='<ul class="width-auto clearfix">';

			    		innerHtml +='	</li>';				    					
			    	}
					if(i == data.list.length){
						innerHtml +='</ul>';
			    	}
			    }
			    $(".footer-floor1").html(innerHtml);
			    loadJQuery();//     layout.js  
		    }
	    });
	});
	function loadJQuery() {
		$('.footer-floor1 > ul > li > .open').on('click', function(){
			$(this).removeAttr('href');
			var elem = $(this).parent('li');
			if (elem.hasClass('on')) {
				elem.removeClass('on');
				elem.find('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.find('div').slideUp();
			}
			else {
				elem.addClass('on');
				elem.children('div').slideDown();
				elem.siblings('li').children('div').slideUp();
				elem.siblings('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.siblings('li').find('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.siblings('li').find('div').slideUp();
			}
		});

		$('a.c5_close.out').click(function(){
			$(this).parents("li").removeClass("on");
		});

		$(".m-dp3-area-right-floor2 a").focus(function(){
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});

		$(".opinion a").focus(function(){
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});


		$(".c5_close").click(function(){
			$(this).attr("href","#none");
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
			$(this).parent().next().find('.open').focus();
			if ( $(this).hasClass('last') ){
				$('.btm-logo > a').focus();
				$(this).hide();
			}
		});
		$(".c5_close").blur(function(){
			$(this).attr("href","#none");
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});
		$('.btm-logo > a').focus(function(){
			$('.c5_close').hide();		
		});
	}
</script>

	<script>
	function ssetCookie( name, value, expirehours ) {
		var todayDate = new Date();
		todayDate.setHours( todayDate.getHours() + expirehours );
	  	document.cookie = name + "=" + escape( value ) + "; path=/; expires=" + todayDate.toGMTString() + ";";
	}
	
	function ccloseWin(popupid) {
		ssetCookie("ncookie"+popupid, "done" , 24 );	
		$("#ncookie"+popupid).hide();
	}
	
	
	
  	function ggetCookie(popupid) {
		cookiedata = document.cookie;
	 	var checkcookie = popupid+"=done";
	 	if (cookiedata.indexOf(checkcookie) > -1){
		 	$("#ncookie"+popupid).hide();
	 	} else {
		 	$("#ncookie"+popupid).show();
	 	}
	}

	function setCookie( name, value, expirehours ) {
		if($("input:checkbox[id='chk_today']").is(":checked") == true){
			var todayDate = new Date();
			todayDate.setHours( todayDate.getHours() + expirehours );
		  	document.cookie = name + "=" + escape( value ) + "; path=/; expires=" + todayDate.toGMTString() + ";";
		}
	}

		    if (dataLength > 0) {

			    		sitename ="";
			    		siteorder ="3";
			    	}else if(dataMap.gubun == 'ETC'){
			    		sitename ="";
			    		siteorder ="4";
			    	}else if(dataMap.gubun == 'DO'){
			    		sitename ="//";
			    		siteorder ="5";
			    	}
			    	if(i == 0){
			    		innerHtml +='<ul class="width-auto clearfix">';
			    	}

			    	if(dataMap.grpend == dataMap.orgorder){
			    		innerHtml +='			</ul>';
			    		innerHtml +='		</div>';
			    		innerHtml +='		<a href="#none" class="c5_close out"><img src="/files/web148/images/main/btn_close_sitemap.png" alt="'+sitename+'  " /></a>';
			    		innerHtml +='	</li>';				    					
			    	}
					if(i == data.list.length){
						innerHtml +='</ul>';
			    	}
			    }
			    $(".footer-floor1").html(innerHtml);
			    loadJQuery();//     layout.js  
		    }
	    });
	});
	function loadJQuery() {
		$('.footer-floor1 > ul > li > .open').on('click', function(){
			$(this).removeAttr('href');
			var elem = $(this).parent('li');
			if (elem.hasClass('on')) {
				elem.removeClass('on');
				elem.find('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.find('div').slideUp();
			}
			else {
				elem.addClass('on');
				elem.children('div').slideDown();
				elem.siblings('li').children('div').slideUp();
				elem.siblings('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.siblings('li').find('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.siblings('li').find('div').slideUp();
			}
		});

		$('a.c5_close.out').click(function(){
			$(this).parents("li").removeClass("on");
		});

		$(".m-dp3-area-right-floor2 a").focus(function(){
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});

		$(".opinion a").focus(function(){
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});


		$(".c5_close").click(function(){
			$(this).attr("href","#none");
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
			$(this).parent().next().find('.open').focus();
			if ( $(this).hasClass('last') ){
				$('.btm-logo > a').focus();
				$(this).hide();
			}
		});
		$(".c5_close").blur(function(){
			$(this).attr("href","#none");
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});
		$('.btm-logo > a').focus(function(){
			$('.c5_close').hide();		
		});
	}
</script>

	<script>
	function ssetCookie( name, value, expirehours ) {
		var todayDate = new Date();
		todayDate.setHours( todayDate.getHours() + expirehours );
	  	document.cookie = name + "=" + escape( value ) + "; path=/; expires=" + todayDate.toGMTString() + ";";
	}
	
	function ccloseWin(popupid) {
		ssetCookie("ncookie"+popupid, "done" , 24 );	
		$("#ncookie"+popupid).hide();
	}
	
	
	
  	function ggetCookie(popupid) {
		cookiedata = document.cookie;
	 	var checkcookie = popupid+"=done";
	 	if (cookiedata.indexOf(checkcookie) > -1){
		 	$("#ncookie"+popupid).hide();
	 	} else {
		 	$("#ncookie"+popupid).show();
	 	}
	}
	</script>

	function getCookie2(emgwordid) {
		cookiedata = document.cookie;
		 var checkcookie = emgwordid+"=done";
		 if (cookiedata.indexOf(checkcookie) > -1){
			 $("#topmost_corona").hide();
		 } else {
			 $("#topmost_corona").show();
		 }
	}
	
	function setCookie( name, value, expirehours ) {
		if($("input:checkbox[id='chk_today']").is(":checked") == true){
			var todayDate = new Date();
			todayDate.setHours( todayDate.getHours() + expirehours );
		  	document.cookie = name + "=" + escape( value ) + "; path=/; expires=" + todayDate.toGMTString() + ";";
		}
	}
	
	function closeWin(emgwordid) {
		if(emgwordid == "topmost_corona"){//jdh  
			setCookie("topmost_corona", "done" , 24 );
		}else{
			setCookie("emgpopupcookie"+emgwordid, "done" , 24 );	
		}
	   	
	 }
	
	'';
	
	function getCookie(emgwordid) {
		cookiedata = document.cookie;
		 var checkcookie = emgwordid+"=done";
		 if (cookiedata.indexOf(checkcookie) > -1){
			 $("#emgpopupcookie"+emgwordid).hide();
		 } else {
			 $("#emgpopupcookie"+emgwordid).show();
		 }
	}

	function loadJQuery() {
		$('.footer-floor1 > ul > li > .open').on('click', function(){
			$(this).removeAttr('href');
			var elem = $(this).parent('li');
			if (elem.hasClass('on')) {
				elem.removeClass('on');
				elem.find('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.find('div').slideUp();
			}
			else {
				elem.addClass('on');
				elem.children('div').slideDown();
				elem.siblings('li').children('div').slideUp();
				elem.siblings('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.siblings('li').find('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.siblings('li').find('div').slideUp();
			}
		});

		$('a.c5_close.out').click(function(){
			$(this).parents("li").removeClass("on");
		});

		$(".m-dp3-area-right-floor2 a").focus(function(){
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});

		$(".opinion a").focus(function(){
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});


		$(".c5_close").click(function(){
			$(this).attr("href","#none");
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
			$(this).parent().next().find('.open').focus();
			if ( $(this).hasClass('last') ){
				$('.btm-logo > a').focus();
				$(this).hide();
			}
		});
		$(".c5_close").blur(function(){
			$(this).attr("href","#none");
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});
		$('.btm-logo > a').focus(function(){
			$('.c5_close').hide();		
		});
	}
</script>

	<script>
	function ssetCookie( name, value, expirehours ) {
		var todayDate = new Date();
		todayDate.setHours( todayDate.getHours() + expirehours );
	  	document.cookie = name + "=" + escape( value ) + "; path=/; expires=" + todayDate.toGMTString() + ";";
	}
	
	function ccloseWin(popupid) {
		ssetCookie("ncookie"+popupid, "done" , 24 );	
		$("#ncookie"+popupid).hide();
	}
	
	
	
  	function ggetCookie(popupid) {
		cookiedata = document.cookie;
	 	var checkcookie = popupid+"=done";
	 	if (cookiedata.indexOf(checkcookie) > -1){
		 	$("#ncookie"+popupid).hide();
	 	} else {
		 	$("#ncookie"+popupid).show();
	 	}
	}
	</script>

	function setCookie( name, value, expirehours ) {
		if($("input:checkbox[id='chk_today']").is(":checked") == true){
			var todayDate = new Date();
			todayDate.setHours( todayDate.getHours() + expirehours );
		  	document.cookie = name + "=" + escape( value ) + "; path=/; expires=" + todayDate.toGMTString() + ";";
		}
	}

			    		sitename ="";
			    		siteorder ="4";
			    	}else if(dataMap.gubun == 'DO'){
			    		sitename ="//";
			    		siteorder ="5";
			    	}
			    	if(i == 0){
			    		innerHtml +='<ul class="width-auto clearfix">';

			    		innerHtml +='	</li>';				    					
			    	}

			    	}
			    }

			    loadJQuery();//     layout.js  
		    }
	    });
	});
	function loadJQuery() {
		$('.footer-floor1 > ul > li > .open').on('click', function(){
			$(this).removeAttr('href');
			var elem = $(this).parent('li');
			if (elem.hasClass('on')) {
				elem.removeClass('on');
				elem.find('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.find('div').slideUp();
			}
			else {
				elem.addClass('on');
				elem.children('div').slideDown();
				elem.siblings('li').children('div').slideUp();
				elem.siblings('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.siblings('li').find('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.siblings('li').find('div').slideUp();
			}
		});

		$('a.c5_close.out').click(function(){
			$(this).parents("li").removeClass("on");
		});

		$(".m-dp3-area-right-floor2 a").focus(function(){
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});

		$(".opinion a").focus(function(){
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});


		$(".c5_close").click(function(){
			$(this).attr("href","#none");
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
			$(this).parent().next().find('.open').focus();
			if ( $(this).hasClass('last') ){
				$('.btm-logo > a').focus();
				$(this).hide();
			}
		});
		$(".c5_close").blur(function(){
			$(this).attr("href","#none");
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});
		$('.btm-logo > a').focus(function(){
			$('.c5_close').hide();		
		});
	}
</script>

	<script>
	function ssetCookie( name, value, expirehours ) {
		var todayDate = new Date();
		todayDate.setHours( todayDate.getHours() + expirehours );
	  	document.cookie = name + "=" + escape( value ) + "; path=/; expires=" + todayDate.toGMTString() + ";";
	}
	
	function ccloseWin(popupid) {
		ssetCookie("ncookie"+popupid, "done" , 24 );	
		$("#ncookie"+popupid).hide();
	}
	
	
	
  	function ggetCookie(popupid) {
		cookiedata = document.cookie;
	 	var checkcookie = popupid+"=done";
	 	if (cookiedata.indexOf(checkcookie) > -1){
		 	$("#ncookie"+popupid).hide();
	 	} else {
		 	$("#ncookie"+popupid).show();
	 	}
	}

	function setCookie( name, value, expirehours ) {
		if($("input:checkbox[id='chk_today']").is(":checked") == true){
			var todayDate = new Date();
			todayDate.setHours( todayDate.getHours() + expirehours );
		  	document.cookie = name + "=" + escape( value ) + "; path=/; expires=" + todayDate.toGMTString() + ";";
		}
	}

	$(document).ready(function() {

		    var dataLength = data.list.length;
		    if (dataLength > 0) {
			    for (var i = 0; i < data.list.length; i++) {
			    	var dataMap = data.list[i];
			    	if(dataMap.gubun == 'KUK'){
			    		sitename ="";
			    		siteorder ="1";
			    	}else if(dataMap.gubun == 'DONG'){
			    		sitename ="";
			    		siteorder ="2";
			    	}else if(dataMap.gubun == 'SI'){
			    		sitename ="";
			    		siteorder ="3";
			    	}else if(dataMap.gubun == 'ETC'){
			    		sitename ="";
			    		siteorder ="4";
			    	}else if(dataMap.gubun == 'DO'){
			    		sitename ="//";
			    		siteorder ="5";
			    	}
			    	if(i == 0){
			    		innerHtml +='<ul class="width-auto clearfix">';
			    	}
			    	if(dataMap.grpstt == dataMap.orgorder){
			    		innerHtml +='	<li><a href="#none" class="open"><span>'+sitename+'</span></a>';
		    			innerHtml +='		<div class="footer-floor1-con absolute'+siteorder+'">';
    					innerHtml +='			<ul class="clearfix">';
			    	}

			    		innerHtml +='			</ul>';
			    		innerHtml +='		</div>';
			    		innerHtml +='		<a href="#none" class="c5_close out"><img src="/files/web148/images/main/btn_close_sitemap.png" alt="'+sitename+'  " /></a>';
			    		innerHtml +='	</li>';				    					
			    	}
					if(i == data.list.length){
						innerHtml +='</ul>';
			    	}
			    }
			    $(".footer-floor1").html(innerHtml);
			    loadJQuery();//     layout.js  
		    }
	    });
	});
	function loadJQuery() {
		$('.footer-floor1 > ul > li > .open').on('click', function(){
			$(this).removeAttr('href');
			var elem = $(this).parent('li');
			if (elem.hasClass('on')) {
				elem.removeClass('on');
				elem.find('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.find('div').slideUp();
			}
			else {
				elem.addClass('on');
				elem.children('div').slideDown();
				elem.siblings('li').children('div').slideUp();
				elem.siblings('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.siblings('li').find('li').removeClass('on');
				elem.siblings('li').find('div').slideUp();
			}
		});

		$('a.c5_close.out').click(function(){
			$(this).parents("li").removeClass("on");
		});

		$(".m-dp3-area-right-floor2 a").focus(function(){
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});

		$(".opinion a").focus(function(){
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});


		$(".c5_close").click(function(){
			$(this).attr("href","#none");
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
			$(this).parent().next().find('.open').focus();
			if ( $(this).hasClass('last') ){
				$('.btm-logo > a').focus();
				$(this).hide();
			}
		});
		$(".c5_close").blur(function(){
			$(this).attr("href","#none");
			$(".footer-floor1-con").slideUp("fast");
			$(".footer-floor1 > ul > li > a").removeClass("on");
		});
		$('.btm-logo > a').focus(function(){
			$('.c5_close').hide();		
		});
	}
</script>

	<script>
	function ssetCookie( name, value, expirehours ) {
		var todayDate = new Date();
		todayDate.setHours( todayDate.getHours() + expirehours );
	  	document.cookie = name + "=" + escape( value ) + "; path=/; expires=" + todayDate.toGMTString() + ";";
	}
	
	function ccloseWin(popupid) {
		ssetCookie("ncookie"+popupid, "done" , 24 );	
		$("#ncookie"+popupid).hide();
	}
	
	
	
  	function ggetCookie(popupid) {
		cookiedata = document.cookie;
	 	var checkcookie = popupid+"=done";
	 	if (cookiedata.indexOf(checkcookie) > -1){
		 	$("#ncookie"+popupid).hide();
	 	} else {
		 	$("#ncookie"+popupid).show();
	 	}
	}
	</script>
